     969             : 
     970             :   /**
     971             :    * Find the aNth occurrence of aName, searching forward if aNth is positive,
     972             :    * and in reverse if aNth is negative (aNth == 0 is invalid), starting from
     973             :    * aFromIndex (not inclusive), and return a 1-based line number.
     974             :    * Also take into account there is an unconditional match at aImplicitLine
     975             :    * unless it's zero.
     976             :    * Return zero if aNth occurrences can't be found.  In that case, aNth has
     977             :    * been decremented with the number of occurrences that were found (if any).
     978             :    *
     979             :    * E.g. to search for "A 2" forward from the start of the grid: aName is "A"
     980             :    * aNth is 2 and aFromIndex is zero.  To search for "A -2", aNth is -2 and
     981             :    * aFromIndex is ExplicitGridEnd + 1 (which is the line "before" the last
     982             :    * line when we're searching in reverse).  For "span A 2", aNth is 2 when
     983             :    * used on a grid-[row|column]-end property and -2 for a *-start property,
